< review>
This place will not last. I mean this in the most pessimistic way. It is a great dive bar, incredible location by the beach. The kind of dive bar you hope will be everywhere you ever go that is nice. And it will be forced out of existence. The lease will run out. And even if a landlord is sympathetic, money will win. Then we'll have another Starbucks or Jamba juice or whatever God forsaken chain place. Enjoy Turc's while you can. It is amazing, and something that you won't be able to experience 10 years from now.<//review>

< review>
My first visit to Turcs was on a Saturday night, and I enjoyed it. When our group of four first arrived there were only a couple other people there, most of whom were seated at the bar, so we ordered a round of drinks and retreated to the corner to play their oversized Jenga set. Several rounds of drinks later, and several rounds of Jenga (most of which I lost) later, we headed out. But the cheap drinks poured by friendly staff meant I came away impressed, and if I'm bar hopping in the area again I definitely intend to stop by for another round (but first I need to practice at Jenga).< /review>

< Text>
My first time here and it definitely won't be my last. I got the avocado & quinoa salad to-go and it was the best salad I've ever had in my life. Super filling, amazing flavors, and a nice little crunch too! I was trying to decide between this salad and the sophisticated salad. The super friendly cashier helped me decide on the avocado salad. She said both were great, but the avocado was the most popular salad and a safer choice, where as the sophisticated salad is more complex. Long story short, I went with the avocado and loved it.

All of the staff I interacted with were so friendly and welcoming. Everyone had a smile on their face and looked genuinely happy to be there.

If you haven't been to Mendocino Farms, GO! & if you haven't tried the avocado & quinoa salad, GET IT!</Text>

Modern farmhouse design and seating, great tasting healthy happy food in the middle of studio City! Awesome. Stop by and check it out. This is worth the stop for food. Not pricey as one might expect. Place your order at the front, you will be given a number pager and moved down the line. While there try a sample of their salad. Once you pay, find a seat and the food will be brought to you. They have a section for kids to sit if they want to play on there own. I like they have filtered water versus tap. I chose the chicken cobb salad with the dressing mixed in while my wife went with the turkey club on a pretzel roll. The taste was amazing. I was truly impressed.<//Review>

We were excited to try Mendocino Farms and found it to be a great newish place with an enthusiastic and friendly staff, and lots of vegetarian, vegan, and gluten-free options.

I had the blue plate special which was half a sandwich and my choice of sides. I had a caprese sandwich which was delicious and very fresh tasting, along with the beet and quinoa side, which was also great and included chunks of green apples (which were a delightful surprise.)

Our kid really enjoyed his grilled cheese sandwich (but he refused to eat the side of apples out of some kind of crazy kid-based non-sensical principle.)

My wife had the Vegan Green Goddess Avocado toast on gluten-free bread. She thought it was good, albeit perhaps a little too much was going on in the dish, so it was hard to identify specifically what was great about it. (It‚Äôs also possible she just wasn‚Äôt in the mood to offer too much of an assessment to further my agenda of being a crazy prolific reviews writer.)

This location offers both Inside and outside seating and it was very crowded on our Sunday afternoon visit, so we had trouble finding the table and ended up crowding together at a table for two. Ultimately this is the sign of a restaurant whose food is worth the visit.

We‚Äôll definitely be back to try the many options available to us with out family‚Äôs various vegetarian, gluten free, and kid-centric diets.<//Text>

< Text>
sandwiches here are tasty and solid.  i always end up going for the pork belly banh mi.  very flavorful and a good lunch size.  the vegetables are crunchy and fresh, and the pork belly is cooked well with good seasoning or marinade.  the panini bread could be a little hotter but that‚Äôs a niggle.

deduct one star for their setup which is an efficiency nightmare.  a person stands at the entrance and takes your order and has to go into excruciating detail explaining the ingredients in the sandwich (which are listed right in front of you) and then you walk down a ramp to pay.

except they have a stand/mini-deli counter setup with their sides and another person asking if you want to try free samples.  which holds up the payment process.

love the food but call ahead and order and skip the line and pick up your food at the other end so you can avoid the dissertation on the ingredients and the sample counter.

oh, and most of the time the person finishing your order at the phone order side will give you the soda for free.<//Text>

Absolutely love this place. it is located on Ventura blvd. at a section were it is not impossible to find parking, even on an evening during the weekend. The food menu reminds somewhat of Lemonade, which is fresh-farm-to-table with a very creative and tasty take on a lot of items. Food ranges form farm raised braised chicken sandwich to pork belly, multiple salad and vegetarian options, and plenty of really good tasting lemonades. Definitely try to check it out if you are on the neighborhood or looking for a place to launch during the week!!< /review>

<Text>My boss orders salads for delivery all the time and raves about this place. OKAY, now I get it.  The place was super busy and packed, but seating was available.  Ranged from people on there lunch breaks, seasoned citizens to a group of moms each with their baby strollers trying to manuever through the dining area.

Since this was my first time here, i wasn't really sure what to get.  They offer a seasonal menu, along with their classics and favorites, as well as vegan options.

It's set up cafeteria style and you order with the hostess.  I asked for a recommendation and the hostess suggested the Peruvian Steak Sandwich.  I was concerned it would be smothered in cheese, so she suggested light cheese.

Near the cashier counter they have fresh made deli items, like pastas and slaws that you can sample.  As I passed down the line you can see all the food being prepared and I noticed some delicious looking bacon bits.

We met Matt, the manager in training.  He came over to say hello and asked if we needed anything, so we asked if we could have a sample of that bacon?  Not only did he give us the bacon bits, but he also gave a us a little taste of some mouth watering make you wanna slap your momma Pork Belly!!  SO GOOD!

The hostess was spot on about my sandwich!! It was so tasty,  you'll see in my pix what's left of my sandwich when I finally remembered to snap a shot.

My co-worker ordered the Modern Tuna "Almost Melt" sandwich with dill pickle potato chips.  I'm purdy sure the sandwich was really good since she wouldn't let the staff take her finished plate because she wanted to eat every crumb and for a second I thought she was going to lick the serving tray to get every morsel of food.

I noticed after that they have a Blue Plate Special which I'm excited to go back to experience other items.  I'll keep you posted of what I discover.

Enjoy!</Text><date>1524628468011</date><Name>Samantha Sanchez</Name>< Pictures>

This place has decent food, but the dumbest system I have seen in a long time.  If you are putting in a to go order or any order for that matter, you put it in with hostess. So the line is out the door and the small entry way is crowded with people. Then you move to another counter where you pay, but here yyou can try different salads to add to your order. Lesson learned, always pre order for quickest in and out.  Staff is friendly.  Atmosphere us nice. Food is tasty. But what a crappy time.<//Review>
